1b1(rgyud): // spya / r+m+maslo/
1b2(rgyud): rgyal po zlog pa maud bya zhes byid/ma pa'i gro'i byuglu tshim mi/sems
1b3(rgyud): ts+tshin rnanus la phan spyod pa smra//rnyog mi rab tu bshed por bya//snang bamyed
1b4(rgyud): cing dpe med pa//tshig gi yul las rnam par 'das//na zhing bdag med
2a1(rgyud): nadag baspyod//mtshan mod mtshan gno rnam par sbyangs//dang gis sangs rgyas la tsun
2a2(rgyud): tshul//mtshan med mtshan gzhi rnam par spangs//khyad par du yang mdor bsdus pas//bdag gis gsal
2a3(rgyud): pabar bshad pa yin//rmos pa rnams la phan 'dod pas//snying rjes 'di ni bstan pa yin//kha cig stong
2a4(rgyud): par 'dod pa dang //kha cig thig le'i gzugs can dang //kha cig khyab 'jug tshul gyis ni//blo dman
2a5(rgyud): dag ni 'jog par byed//de nyid nges par yang dag par//rgyu yi gnas kyi spyod yul nyid//rgyu dang 'bras bu
2b1(rgyud): mu grub na//bsgoms pa med cing byang chub myed//rgyu yi yid ches spangs pa 'di//thog ma tha ma med pa'i bdag/sgyu ma'i
2b2(rgyud): shosaM las drang ba//rnam pa sna tshogs ston par bye dri//khyo cig drag po'i rang bzhin du//kha cig zhing chen po che//
2b3(rgyud): cig phyag rgya'i rang bzhi ni gzugs//khyi cig 'dor zhing g.yo ba dang //glu gar de bzhin sel snyan dang //lU yi sngags ni brjod
2b4(rgyud): pa nyid//kho cig sngags ni yang dag dgod//kha cig dkyil 'khor bre ba dang //dbang la sogs pa brtag pa dang //'byung dang
2b5(rgyud): 'byung las gyur pa'i lus//de ltar la stsogs mtha' yos mchog/sangs rgyas la sogs rdo rje brtags//gang che sems
2b6(rgyud): ni legs gnas pa//de bzhin nyid kyi spyod yul nyid//dkyil 'khor de bzhin 'gyur ba ni//phan 'dod rnams kyis shes
3a1(rgyud): par bya//phung po la sogs tshogs rnams kyis//gang zhig khyad par gyis bcos pa//lus drug yid
3a2(rgyud): gsum bcos pa'i phyir//rdul chen dkyil 'khor zhes byar gsungs//phung sogs gzhan sogs mthong ba'i phyir//tshogs kyi
3a3(rgyud): kyil 'khor zhes byor gsungs//sems kyi dkyil 'khor dag pa ste//rang bzhin med par bsgoms par bya//me long lta bu'i
3a4(rgyud): gcig nyid//dang po grur ni rtogs par bya//so sor rtog pa zhes gsungs pas//shar gyi grur ni rnam par rgyan//bya ba nun
3a5(rgyud): tan khyad 'phags pa//byang gi zur ni rnam par spros//mnyam nyid ye shes chen po ni//bag chags med gro rjes rtogs byed//
3a6(rgyud): gzhan du'ang dkyil 'khor gru bzhi pa//grwa yi dbus ni thams cad du//de nyid 'di ni rab 'jug pas//ye shis spyod yul du
3b1(rgyud): ni bad+hAg/sgo bzhir yang dag brjod pa ni//de bzhin dran pa bzhir byung ba//de bzhin gra bzhir gsungs pa ni//sbyin pa bzhi ni rnam dag pa//dbus
3b2(rgyud): su dkyil 'khor gzugs ni//mi bskyod pa yi rnam par rkyen//zhi dang chos don rgyan pa lngas//de dag thams cad dkyil 'khor 'grub//dra ba dra pyid
3b3(rgyud): zla ba sogs//dkyil 'khar du ni bris pa dang //rta babros la sogs thams cad ni//ting 'dzin yan lag rta babs nyid//sems kyi mthar thug brjod
3b4(rgyud): pa ste/de nyid rang bzhin las ni gsungs//gang zhig sems kyi rab 'phel ba//ting 'dzin yan lag rnam par gnas//de nyid dra ba zhesu gsungs//
3b5(rgyud): dA ba phyed pa phyed du ste/dril bu do shal brtag pa ni//rang gi btsun mo rtogs par byed//sgra brnyan rnam pa lta bur ni//chos rnams thams cad so sor
3b6(rgyud): TIgaso//chos rnams ma skyes mthong ba'i phyir//de nyid rgyal mtshani phreng bar gsungs//bla re la sogs gang bres pa//dngos po la sogs dang po nges//
3b7(rgyud): sems ni bla re zhes byar bshod//dam pa'i don las gsungs pa'o//gos dreng de dag thams cad ni//rnam pa sna tshogs snang ba nyid//gang zhig rdo rje
4a1(rgyud): rnam seMs / so shes sa mdza//de la gtu rgyug lkug sa//glu ma rnams ni thams dang//
4a2(rgyud): shes ngas rnam pa //sgrub sa rnaMs nyid la khyer du ni sgyus//mug nugs na ster//rnam pag mi
4a3(rgyud): tu mtshan nyid med//bla ma slong ma rnams gsal ba'o//rab tu 'jug pa de nyid gsungs//sbyin steg/ying ni ba shed pa yang //lha rnams tshim pa yi
4a4(rgyud): rjod/rnamartog ma pa'i sems gang ni//brag du sgra yis mtshan ma // brag sa minang du//gzugs kyi rung sags sde pa rnams//ma
4a5(rgyud): // //btsun kyi sa nga / n-i gags//de ltar rgyu smin
4a6(rgyud): bshid nas ni//rab tu gnas pa rjod pa da//sku gsung thugs la N+Di rgyuni//ga shig sems ni stan byung //de nyid satu gnas par brjod/
4b1(rgyud): phung po rnams kyi dngos po ca//gang zhig sngags kyi mtshan nyin na//ngan gsal bar brjod par bya//yid rnams kyis ni skad du yang //gang zhig gsang ba bdag gis brjod//
4b2(rgyud): skye ba med cing snang med pa//mtshan gzhi mtshan nyid rnam par spangs//gsung ba'i don ni rtogs pa'i phyir//'di ni nga yis sngagasu gsungs//sngags ni gsal ba rab shad
4b3(rgyud): nos ni//lha rnams yang ni brjod par bya//phung po khams dang skye mched kyi//rang bzhin gyi ni legs gnas gang //yang dag byang chub zer pa nyid//de kun yang dgar
4b4(rgyud): brtags shing //gal te sems kyis nyer brtags gang //lho zhes bya bar yang dag bshad//sku gsung thugs kyi phyag rgya la so//de nyid du ni yang dag gsungs//lha la
4b5(rgyud): gsol btab rnal 'byor ni//gsal bar ngo yis brjod par bya//de nas skyil krung bcas nas ni//sna yi rtse mor bltos nas kyang //rang gi rang bzhin rnal 'byor
4b6(rgyud): gyis//de nyid mthong bar bzhag par bya//snying ka'i gnas su lag pa gnyis//'bad pas mnyam par sbyar na su//mi rtog pa yi rang bzhin du//gang tshe sems ni//
4b7(rgyud): rang rgyu ba//sangs rgyas thams cad 'dus pa'i bdag/de tshe de la skye bar 'gyur//sangs rgyas thams cad 'dus pa'i bdag/myur bar byin gyis rlob par 'gyur//
5a1(rgyud): sangs rgyas thams cad 'dus pa'i bdag sangs rgyas kun gyi rtog pa'i bdag/thugs kyi rdo rjes gsungs pa bzhin//rnal 'byar sangs rgyas thams cad 'gyur//nga yis gsal ba
5a2(rgyud): brjod pa ni//sku gsung thugs kyi grub sbyin pa//sangs rgyas kun mchog gsang ba'i don//thabs dang shes rab spyod yul don//sems cad don du snying rje che//sangs rgyas byang chub rab sgrub pa//
5a3(rgyud): snartsi dkyil 'khor dA yis gsungs//de dag thams cad dbyibs tsam du//mdor bsdus thams cad ma byas so//res 'ga' dam tshig 'khor lo yang //de nyid zhes bya ma gsungs//rtogs//
5a4(rgyud): bib cung zad tsam gyis ni//gang 'grub de ni raM 'ga' yang //gsung gi 'khor lorwa gsungs pa yin//rnam rtog med par lhar mos pas//sgrub po dam pas bsgrub par bya//khrag dang khu ba de bzhin
5a5(rgyud): shar ba shi dang ni gci ba nyid//dam tshig zhes bya rab 'bad par//gang zhig bdag gis tshig gsungs pa//de rnams kun la de bzhin gshegs//de rnams tha snyad tsam gyis gnas//gung
5a6(rgyud): dam tshig 'dod chags sems//des ni de nyid rab tu spyod//gang tshe sems ni chags gyur pa//de ni sems can yod ma yin//de la kun tu rtog pa yi//khrag ni za bar 'gyur ba'o//khrag ni chen po
5a7(rgyud): zos nas ni//'od dpag med pa'ang bza' bar bya//gang zhig chos rnams las skyes pa//khu ba'i sgrar ni bsregs par bya//de tshe ma skyes rtogs pa'i phyir//bza' bar yang dag gsungs pa nyid//
5b1(rgyud): dngos po kun gyi mnyam pa nyid//sha chen du ni rab tu dbye//mi dmigs pa yi rnal 'byor gyis//bza' ba zhes byu mngon par 'arjod//gang zhig rab tu 'dzag pa'i sems//nus pa'i rjes su sbyor ba las//phyag rgyu las rgyu
5b2(rgyud): yis//de yang gci ba'i sgra yis brjod//chos dang chos min nges pa'i sems//sbas pa'i tshad ni gnas pa 'di//chos rnams thams cad rab rtogs pa'o//bshad pa za bar yang dag 'arjod//dam tshig nyid kyi mtshan nyid ni//
5b3(rgyud): rnams thams cad gsal bar bshad//'di rnams don ni rtogs pa yis//sangs rgyas kun gyi bdag nyid 'gyur//dpal bde ba dam pa rtogs par byed pa dang ldan pa zhes bya ba'i rgyud byin gyis brlab pa'i rim pa chen po
5b4(rgyud): mkha' 'gro ma dra ba sdom pa'i brtag pa rnyog pa med pa zhes bya ba rdzog so////rgya gar gyi mkhan po paN+Di ta ga ya d+ha ra dang /bod kyi lo ts+tsha ba dge slong shAkya ye shes kyis bsgyur ba'o////rgya gar skad du/
5b5(rgyud): sa bud+d+ha ka pA la nA ma yo gi nI tan+t+ra ra dze/bod skad du/dpal sangs rgyas thod pa zhes bya ba rnal 'byor ma'i rgyud kyi rgyal po//dpal sangs rgyas thod pa la phyag 'tshal lo//'di skad bdag gis thos pa dus gcig ni/
5b6(rgyud): bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi sku dang /gsung dang /thugs rdo rje'i dkyil 'khor chen po rgyan dang ldan pa'i dbus su//de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad dang //rnal 'byor ma rnams dang lhan ces
5b7(rgyud): tu bzhugs te//'phags pa kun dga' bo la sogs pa 'dod chags dang bral ba'i gtso bo rnams dang /'phags pa sbyin ras gzigs dbang phyug la sogs pa'i byang chub sems dpa' bye ba phrag brgyad cu dang /
6a1(rgyud): yang thabs cig tu bzhugs so//de nas bcom ldan 'das kyis rdo rje'i tshig gis rdo rje chen po'i gnas su//rgyud thams cad dang sngags yang dag par bshad nas/de bzhin
6a2(rgyud): gshegs pa thams cad kyi bdag pos rdo rje dang pad+mo yang dag par sbyar bas/btsun mo'i b+ha ga ra yongs su mya ngan las 'das so//de yongs su mya ngan las 'dras pa mthong nas/byang chub
6a3(rgyud): sems dpa' thams cad dang /rnal 'byor ma thams cad rmad du gyur te cig la cig lta zhing /e ma'o bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi bdag po dkyil 'khor chen po
6a4(rgyud): rgyun dang ldan pa'i dbus su ji ltar yongs su mya ngan las 'das/de nas rnal 'byor ma sna tshogs sde ma la byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po phyag na rdo rjes 'di skad ces gsol to//lha
6a5(rgyud): mo sems can bsod nams dman pa rnams nus pa la zhon par 'gyur ba'i thabs cung zad mchis sam//gsungs pa/rnal 'byor gyi rgyud la bye ba phrag drug nyid do//rnal 'byor ma'i rgyud la ni bye ba
6a6(rgyud): phrag bcu drug nyid do//mdo sde so so la ni bye ba phrag brgyad cu'o//de bzhin du pha rol tu phyin pa'i theg pa ni bye ba la bsgres pa'i 'bum phrag lnga'o//'di dag thams cad ni thub pa'i dbang pos
6a7(rgyud): gsungs so//sngags dang bral na ni rgyud kyis nas pa mi snang ste//rgyud la la ri ni ci nas sngags bye ba bzlas par gsungs so//bsod nams 'bring po rnams kyis ni sngags 'bum pas myur bar
6b1(rgyud): /'grub par gsungs so//bsod nams che bas shin tu myur bar 'grub pa'o//de ltar rdo rje chen po rgyud kyi bdag po'i gtso bos gsungs so//bsod nams chung ba'i sems can rnams kyis na
6b2(rgyud): bye ba bzlas par gsungs so//sems can 'bad rtsol chung ba rnams kyis ni 'bum bzlas par bdage smra'o//sems can sgom pa la zhan pa rnams kyis ni khri kho na bzlas par bya'o//sems can 'dod
6b3(rgyud): tshogs le zhugs pa rnams kyi bzlas pa ji ltar lags//blun po dang lkugs pa'i rigs can rnams kyi sngags kyi grangs ji ltar lags//shin tu dmigs pa'i sngags kyis bzlas pa ji ltar lags//
6b4(rgyud): 'di ltar phan tshun smra bas bzlas na dngos grub gzhan du yang 'gyur ro//gal te dman pa'i sems kyis nyon mongs bzhin pas bzlas pa de'i tshe bskal pa skar ma lta bur yang de la dngos grub med/
6b5(rgyud): nga de ltar thos nas rnal 'byor ma sna tshogs snga ma bcom ldan 'das kyis zhal la lta bar byed cing zur mig dang bcas pa'i chags pas bltas te/shin tu khro bas 'jigs par byed cing snying
6b6(rgyud): rdorje'i thugs 'khrugs pas/bdud kyi dpung rab tu bcom mo//de ltar bzhugs pa'i lha mo chen mo rgyud thams cad kyi bdag po'i dbang phyug la de nas des gzigs pa tsam gyis bcom ldan 'das
6b7(rgyud): kyis dbulas sngags phyung ngo //oM bud+d+he sid+d+he su sid+d+he/a mri ta a ra dze bud+d+ha ka pA la s+pho Ta ne s+pho Ta ya tA sa ya ho hUM phaT//de ltar sngags kyi mchog son pas sa rim pa bdun gyi 'og tu chud
7a1(rgyud): pa'i klu rnams bcom par byas shing phye mar byas nas slar 'ongs te sna tshogs sde ma'i zhal du zhugs te/pad+ma'i nang nas byung nas slar thod par zhugs so//sngags 'di'i mthus klu
7a2(rgyud): rnams zhig ste/skrag cing rdul byung bar 'gyur ro//nor rgyas la sogs pa'i rdzu 'phrul chen po'i klu thams cad lhags te/stobs kyi rgyu dang /dung skyong dang /'jog po dang /mtha' yas dang /pad+ma
7a3(rgyud): chen po la sogs pa klu chen po rnams dang /gzhan gang yang rung ba dug las byung ba thams cad kyang lhags so//rnal 'byor ma sna tshogs sde ma lo kha phyogs te klu thams cad kyis zhus pa/lha
7a4(rgyud): mo bka' stsol ci gzhig bgyi zhes smra'o//gsungs pa/gang yang sangs rgyas nyams su myong ba de ltar gyis shig/de ltar thos pa tsam gyis dkyil 'khor chen po rgyan dang ldan pa'i dbus su
7a5(rgyud): bcom ldan 'das kyis thod pa kha phye ba te glegs bam byung ngo //nam mkha' la sgra byung ngo //lha mo sna tshogs sde ma bzung //sems can kun la phan 'dogs ma//rgyud 'di rgyal po chen po ste//rnal 'byor
7a6(rgyud): ma yi gong na med//sangs rgyas thod pa zhes bya ba//sems can kun la phan+da byed pa'o//de ltar thos nas sna tshogs sde mas glegs bam yang dag par gzung ste//phyag na rdo rje la nye bar btang ngo //phyog
7a7(rgyud): na rdo rjes rgyud 'di zung //sems can kun la bde 'bab pa//rnal 'byor ma yi dngos grub ku na//'bras bu myur du ster byed pa'o//mnan drang spar ba ye shes che//gong na med pa rnyed dka' ba//gsang ba
7b1(rgyud): mchog gi nyams dga' ba//lus kun la ni rnam par gnas//na mkha' lding dang char dbab dang //dngul chu bcud kyis len pa dang //bskrad dang dbang du bya nyid dang //rmongs drung mngon spyod nyid dang ni//
7b2(rgyud): /dpung la sogs pa rengs nyid dang //dus su zin pa bzlog pa dang //phur bus gdab dang bsad pa dang //rtag tu sgrub pa byed pa dang //sna tshogs sngags rims ji bzhin dang //ji bzhin rnal 'byor ma bskyed dang //
7b3(rgyud): dpal chen he ru ka yi ni//dus su zin pa bzlog pa dang //bskyed pa dang ni gnas brgyad dang //dngos dang dngos med spros mod dang //srid par spyod cing dgos med dang //dgongs pas bshad pa mchog chen dang //
7b4(rgyud): rnal 'byor ma yi mchog chen dang //rnal 'byor ma yi 'dus pa dang //nus pa rnam pa mang gsungs pa//thos pa tsam gyis 'grub par 'gyur//gzugs brnyan dag pa nyid dang ni//de bzhin bsten pa skyong ba
7b5(rgyud): dang //dur khrod 'jigs pa cha bzang dang //ro langs sgrub pa la sogs dang //stobs po che rnams dgug pa dang //de bzhin 'jig rten gsum dgug dang //rims kyis gdung ba 'jig rten dang //dgro yi
7b6(rgyud): kha sogs bcing ba dang //de bzhin bsad dang bslu ba deng //mi snang byed pa mchog dang ni//mig sman dang ni ril bu nyid//bcud len ral gri nyid dang ni//sangs rgyas thod pa'i sbyor ba yis//thos pa tsam
7b7(rgyud): gyis 'grub par 'gyur//mi snang ba ni mchog cheni dang //sna tshogs sgyu 'phrul rnam 'phrul dang //rang gi gzugs ni bsgyur ba dang //gzhan gyi lus la gzhug sogs dang //sangs rgyas bye bas rab bsrungs/
8a1(rgyud): pA li//sa sa rgyas sum ga chen rnams//zlos pa tsam gyis 'gra rgyas byed//gnan da/thos kyu smrig dgos//mog 'phrul byed pa nyid do so//ga \u0f7fna rnam pa mAng she/
8a2(rgyud): pa 'dod pa lnga ni bsten bzhin pas//'di ru 'grub par gdon mi zu//'jigs shing 'joms pa'i tshad chen po//gcig gis 'bum las rgyal ba dbyud //skyes pa gcig gis 'dod chen gyis/
8a3(rgyud): bud med 'bum phrag 'jig byed cing //rdo rjer byed pa rnyed dga' ba//gcig gis thams cad 'do ba spyad// nas gzhan yang rab ba shad pa//mkhar lding sbyor ba ro ma ji bzhin//rgyud kun dri yang rnyed ga
8a4(rgyud): ga/su ga sa rnams kyi tshul min gyi//rgyud kun du yang ma sus s+ho//sas rgyas byed pa'i gzung nge bzhin//rdo rje mgon pos gsus pa yi//me ng+ge'i'aM lding shin tu rmad byu y-i/ rten /
8a5(rgyud): narnyed da/'a ba'i//sbyor ba rnam pa bco rgyang gsungs//shU li kA yi sbyor ba dang //reg pa 'dzin dang rgyan po'i gyeng //rnga rngu zung med 'brog pa dang //shin brdzun zhugs pas 'ching bra dang //khwa byug+sa/
8a6(rgyud): dkris 'byed pa dang //stegs byed chu thugs dung 'jung da //zod lo kor 'phrog sbyin pa dang //ras g.yog bal lcags brdab pa dang //yig gsum bsam garten gyis ni gtam//'di rnams kyisan
8a7(rgyud): 'jug pa //mnga' lding byur ba'i ci brgyad po//'jig rten gsuman pa rnyed do//2//sems can rnams la phan byed pa//rdo rje mnan po nyid kyis gsus//de nas gzhan yang ma shid pa//ma/
8b1(rgyud): gi ye shes ji bzhin pa//b+ha ga'i dbus su rnam par bzhugs//bde ba chen po steng byed pa//'di nyid du ni kun gnas kyang //byis pa rmongs pas mi shes so//der ni bcud dang bcud len te//de nyid du ni sangs rgyas bzhugs//
8b2(rgyud): de ni dkyil 'khor bzang po'o//der ni slob ma dbang bskur ba'o//der ni he ru ka dpa'o//nyi shu rtsa bzhi'i dbang gtso bo//deH ni na mkha' lding 'jigs pa//de nyid du na ro langs sgrub//der ni dur khrod brgyad po
8b3(rgyud): rnams//skad cig tsam gyis bskyed pa'i rgyu//der ni sangs rgyas bdag nyid te//stong phrag gsum ni rnam par bzhugs//deng ni 'jig rten khams kun te//de nyid bcom ldan 'das lha mo//sangs rgyas la
8b4(rgyud): sogs bskyed pa'i yum//byang chub sems dpa' dpal chen po//shes rab pha rol phyin dpung panyen//de nyid bsod nams kun ster ma//de nyid thar pa ste dbyed ma//phyag rgya chen po grags chen po//dngos
8b5(rgyud): grub kun ni 'dod byed ma//ma dang tshangs mo sring mo dang //bu mo bud med rab brtan ma//shes rab mnyes shing 'jigs byed ma//'gro drug bde sdug bag chags bcas//'khor ba mya ngan 'das nyid dang //
8b6(rgyud): bdag nyid chen po de nyid de//rnam rtog kun tu rtog pa nyid//de bzhin 'char dang nub pa dang //nyin mtshan ma la bstan bza' ba dang //nges pa'i brertul zhugs rtsis dang grangs//rnam par mi rtog yang
8b7(rgyud): dag rtog/dman dang mchog dang bar ma dang //gzhan dang gang dang de dang ni//de nyid bdag nyid chen po gcig/sems can kun la bde ba 'bab//de ltar thos nas phyag na rdo rje la sogs pa'i byang chub
9a1(rgyud): gsol to//e ma lo//sna tshogs sde marnal 'byor mo//sems can kun la bad 'bab ma//glegs pas don dang lda na gang shig/de ni sangs rgyas byin rlangs be shad //de nas phyag ni rdo rje'i phyag gnyis
9a2(rgyud): glang po che'i lag pa lhu rar tu brjed ste/glegs pam yang dag par blangs so//de nas sangs rgyas kyi byin rlabs kyis phyag rgya chen po'i rdo rje'i gnas bu den dang bcas pa'i gzhung slob gyur to//phyag na
9a3(rgyud): rdo'i b+hir+ya/nas byu ste//sna tshogs sde ma'i zub su sa pa'o//de nas myen na rdo gi spyod sbyin bye ban ma chen pasanal 'byo mtshan ma la 'di sa dgasol to//sngags kyi rnam pa gang nig yogs/
9a4(rgyud): gas nimaseM ste jug/na du sbyin pa gang na sa rnas/ snyid sgrub pa das pad // sa chu lan sa pa//dus 'i ste byed gang nig las/
9a5(rgyud): 'ang rgya // chen po rdo lnga su//rnal 'gye ma mi rnam ngas kyi//gsus pa/rgyud 'dir sngon du brten pa meng//de bzhin yul dang dus chos dang //gar de rgyun rgya ming /
9b1(rgyud): dang ldan pas rtag tu brten//dusu dang bya ba'i dus mi bya//sangs rgyas thad pa'i sbyor ba yis//bros pa tsam gyis 'grub par 'gyur//sangs rgyas rdo rje zhes su gsungs//thod pa phru gsum yang dag 'brum/
9b2(rgyud): grasang bar gnas pa'i rtsa//de yi sna tshogs ngo mtshor byed//sde ni 'de chen ye shes so//'di nyid theg po chen po ste//rnal 'byor ma yi rtsa las byung //de ni rmad byung che mchog ste//sangs rgyas thod pa'i sbyor ba
9b3(rgyud): nyid//de nyid he ru ka dpa'o//'khor ba'i 'jigs las sgrol byed pa//sangs rgyas thod pa'i sbyor ba yis//sangs rgyas kun gyi bde ba 'bab//rnal 'byor chen mo sna tshogs bde//dpa' dang bdag mo dbong
9b4(rgyud): phyug ma//de yi thod pa'i dkyil 'khor la//sngags dang rgyud ni rnam par gnas//de yi ye shes bzang po ni//lhan cig skyes pa dag las 'byung //de ni rigs pa'i dbang lnga dang //sangs rgyas bdun
9b5(rgyud): mtshan can te//sna tshogs sbyor dang tshe 'phel dang //dngos grub thams cad sgrub pa ni//sangs rgyas thod pa'i myong ba yis//'grub par 'dir ni gdon mi ze//man ngag lam las gang shes pa//bla ma'i
9b6(rgyud): drin las shes par bya//sangs rgyas thod pa'i rgyud chen po rnal 'byor ma rnams kyi gong na med pa gsang ba'i yang shin tu gsang ba zhes bya ba las dngos grub thams cad dang ye shes btan la dbab pa dang /

11a1(rgyud): dag ni sangs rgyas rnams kyis kyang shin tu rnyed par dka'o//thal ba de dang rdo rje gtsug gis byug par byas nas//ji srid du lus la mtshon chas phog pa de srid du mi tshugs so//slar zhing
11a2(rgyud): dgra thams cad kyi mgo bo 'chad par 'gyur ro//gang sdang ba la bltas na de long bar 'gyur ro//gang zhig sdang ba'i sems 'dzin pa skyo bar 'gyur ro//thal ba de nyid dang mar khu bzang pos mig byugasran
11a3(rgyud): dag tshad stong mthong bar 'gyur ro//gang ci yang rung ba sa'i 'og na gnas pa'i gter dpag tshad stong gi 'og tu son pa'i dngul dang gser dang rin po tshwa gang na yod pa de thams cad la srin lag gis
11a4(rgyud): bsdigs mdzu byas pa cam gyis thams cad mdun du lhags te gsol ba 'deb so//kyis sa rgyas thod pa'i rnal 'byor pa gter ldong la sems can gyi don gyis shig/de gter blangs na gang 'dod

11a6(rgyud): gang 'dod pa de byed do//bkrus pa tsam gyis langs par 'dri la TI tsam med do//bral ba de dben nye'i phye ma dang bsgos te cig tu byas la/rdo rje'i gtsug rjes su byin te khab len gyi lcags kyi phye ma
11a7(rgyud): bsre shing gised kyi phyi ma yang cung zad bsre bar bya'o//rdo rje'i chu'i khu ba dang lhan cig tu bsngos te ba so ma'i snod du nyi ma bdun gyi bar du shig go//de nas 'khris pa chen po mnyas te ta khrag dang /
11b1(rgyud): lhan cig tu bsnon la yang snod de nyid du nyi ma gsum bzhag par bya'o//de nas gton te lcags kyi snod du bzhag par bya'o//zangs ma'i snod du bzhag pa de med mang du bcug na gser dang dngul du 'gyur bar sdom
11b2(rgyud): nyi med do//srangad gcig kyang snang stong gA rin thar du 'gyur te rin po che dang 'dra bar 'gyur ro//gser da ma sha cig dang dngul srang cig bsres te me la bzhun srang sum brgya'i thang gi tshad du 'gyur bar 'di
11b3(rgyud): la the tsom med do//'di lta bu'i sbyor ba ni sangs rgyas rnams kyis kyang rnyed par dka'o//'jig rten dbang phyug la sogs pa'i byang chub sems dpa' grags pa chen po snying rje dang ldan pa'i bdag nyid chen po
11b4(rgyud): stobs che ba de rnams kyis kyang sbyin par mi nus so//'di yi sbyor ba rnyed dka' ba//sangs rgyas thod po'i rgyud du gsung //rgyud gzhan rnams su smras pa yin//'dus sogs rnal 'byor rgyud du ni//sbyor ba
11b5(rgyud): rnam pa ma gsungs pa//gang tshe sngon du bsnyen de'i tshe//de yi sbyor bas ci zhig bya//bsod nams dman pa'i sems can gang //mtshams med lnga ni byed pa yang //sangs rgyas thod ba'i sbyor ba yin//'di lta'i
11b6(rgyud): sbyor ba 'grub par 'gyur//dngos po de yis blo chen rnams//sems can don la gcig tu brtson//srang cig gis bsres bye ba'i rin//sbyor ba kun tu rnyed par dka'//sbyor ba glegaso ba ma la mi bri//
11b7(rgyud): blablo ma'i drin las//sa par bya//bla mas dngos grub bla mas thar//bla ma ston pa rnams kun pa//des na slob ma blo can gyis//'bad pas bla mo mnyes par bya//thal ba de nyid kyis ltas lta ba'i don du bu mo'i
12a1(rgyud): mgo la thugs te rdo rje gtsug gis bumo bkru'o//yang thal ba'i thig le byas la//tshangs pa rdo rjes maN+Dal gru ba ni byas te//de'i dbus su bu mo bzhag par bya'o//bdug spos lngas/
12a2(rgyud): bdugs shing sangs rgyas thams cad kyis byin gyis brlabs na bu mo la 'bab par 'gyur te//'das pa dang /ma 'ongs pa dang da ltar byung ba ston to//bu don gyis 'bras la sngags 'di lan bdun du mngon
12a3(rgyud): par sngag so//oM bud+d+ha ka pA li ni de hi//de hi da dA pa ya da dA pa ya he he b+ha ga ba ti shI g+h+raM khad gaM d+ha ra hi bud+d+ha kA pA la badz+ra s+ya yadz+nyA ma laM g+hA ya hUM staM hri phaT a phaT/yungs kar snun pa tsam gyis ni//
12a4(rgyud): bu mo grags chen ma ni dpyod//de yi kha nas ral gri bdun//'byung ba la ni the tsom med//sangs rgyas thod pa'i rnal 'byor skad cig ma de nyid la 'grub par 'dir som nyid med do//de ltar ral gcing
12a5(rgyud): grub pas bye ba brgya stong gi rig 'dzin 'grub par bskur bar 'gyur ro//'di lta bu'i sbyor ba ni 'jig rten gsum na yang rnyed par dka'o//bu mo bkrus pa tsam gyis rnal 'byor mar 'gyur ro//de'i
12a6(rgyud): thal ba lcags gsum gyis bkris te ril bu byas nas khang bcug pa tsAm gyis ni mi snang bar 'gyur ro//shes rab can gyis smram cu pa yang bskor ro//sangs rgyas thams cad kyis kyang mi gcig
12a7(rgyud): po//ril bu lag par blangs pas dngos po gang dang gang la reg pa tsam gyis de dbang du 'gyur ro//thal ba'i sbyor ba'i 'di dag ni//sangs rgyas kyis kyang rnyed par dka'//oM bud+d+ha ka pA la rje hU~M
12b1(rgyud): oM bAdzig rten gsum sgrub pa'i sngagaso//oM bAd+d+ha ka pA li ni hrIHhU~M/dgra brlag pa'i sngags s+ho//oM mAhA ka pA la badz+rI kha kha khA ha khA ha sarba duSh+TA na b+ha g+ha g+hA ta ya g+hA t+yA ya sarba sha truM oM ha tri hU~M phaT//badz+ra

12b3(rgyud): le'u skye gnyis pa'o///de nas byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po phyag na rdo rjes sna tshog sde sko ma la btud de/'di skad ces gsol to//sems can don la gcig brtson pa//
12b4(rgyud): sngal chos bcom ldan 'das lha mo//'di lha'i rab tu sbyor zhes pa//rgyud gzhan dag tu ma gsungs shing //sangs rgyas kun gyis rab sbas pa//de ni 'bad de gsal bar mdzod//lha mo chen mo khyod
12b5(rgyud): kyis gsungs//lha yi le'u dri ji lta bu//sangs rgyas thod pa rnal 'byor ma'i//rgyud du lha rnams du zhig gsungs//de ru gzugs ni ji lta bu//gum pa yis ni nyan par 'tshal//gsungs pa/raM las nyi ma
12b6(rgyud): rma na par bya//nyi ma'i steng du hU~M byu nga'i//rdo rje nag po sreg pa'i bad//rdo rje de nyid 'odadi zer gyis//rabyu d+hU ba'i mtshanas bcing de//de bzhin rdo rje nang byung ba//rdo rjes gzhi bsdam par+yA bA//rdo rje'i sag zhi'i
12b7(rgyud): rlung bar//e yi rnam pa bdag nyid che//gru gsum khams gsum bdag nyid can//yi ge lam gyur sa yin//dkyil 'khor gru ba zhi rab ser po'o//de la dbus nas sa bon ni//yi go oM ste chos bdag nyid/dkri//
13a1(rgyud): /oM las byung ba'i 'khor lo ni//rtsa rnams kun gyi rang bzhin can//rnal 'byor ma ni rnam par bzhugs//rdza ni drug cu la rgyan dang //sprul pa drug cu rtsa bani 'dab//des na rtsa brgya nyi shu'o//rdo rje sku
13a2(rgyud): yis bdag nyid che/shes rab can gyis de ltar bsam//de yi dbus gnas sa bon ni//baM dkar yi ge las byung ba//chu yi dkyil 'khor zlum po'o//rtswa rnams thams cad chu yi ni//dkyil 'khor la ni thim par
13a3(rgyud): 'gyur/slar yang bsam par bya ba ni//rab dmar las byung me'i dkyil 'khor//gru gsum 'bar ba'i bdag nyid can//rab tu 'bar bzhin pa yi ni//rtsa ba'i 'khor lo yang dag blta//de nas bsam par bya ba
13a4(rgyud): ni//yaM gyur rlung gi dkyil 'khor ni//zla ba phyed pa'i rnam 'dra sngo//rtsa rnams rab tu g.yo ba'i gzugs//thim gyur 'khor lo'i rig par gsungs//de dag thams cad thim gyur pa//de yi dbus gnas rnal
13a5(rgyud): 'byor pa//de ltar shes par byed gang zhig/sangs rgyas thod pa'i rnal 'byor pas//de nas zla ba bsam par bya//zla ba'i steng du nyi ma'o//de yi dbus chud sa bon ni//hUM dang a yi rang bzhin no//yi ge ka yis
13a6(rgyud): rgyun ste/ka ni ha la thim par 'gyur//mi phyed pa yi ha dang hUM//gnyi ga'i bdag nyid can blta'o//h+ya ni mi shigs shes rab kyi//bdag nyid u dang yi ge dag/gnyi ga gcig tu gyur pa ni//yi ge hUM ge chos

13b2(rgyud): rlabs//sa don rdo nA las byung ba//dpa' bo khrag 'thung mdog sngon po//zhal gcig pa la phyag bzhi pa//gtso bo hUM zhes 'don pa ste//skyil krung phyed pa'i gar gyis gnas//gnyi ga'ang khro ba'i bdag nyid can/
13b3(rgyud): stag gi lpags pa'i na gza' banabs//mgo ba rlon pa'i phreng ba 'chang //bsegasu mchod phyir thogs pa yi//shin tu gzhad pas 'jigs che ba'i//gtso bo snying rje'i bdag nyid blta//da rung rgyan mgu
13b4(rgyud): do 'khor gdub dang //gtsar bu rus pa'i ska rags 'ching //g.yer ka bcas pa'i rkang gdub can//ma lus bdud rnams 'joms par byed//ral pa'i gcod pan yang dag ldan//sangs rgyas rnam pa lnga'i yas
13b5(rgyud): rgyan//zla ba phyed pa 'dzin pa'i lha//dbu la sna tshogs rdo rjes mnan//'khor lo rna cha gdu bu dang //phyag rgya rnam pa lnga yis mtshan//thal ba'i rdul can 'jigs par byed//thod pa gti mug gis rgyan pa'i

13b7(rgyud): bde ba kun gyi gzugs can ma//phyag gnyis sgra ni grol ba'o//he ru ka las 'khyud gnas ma//de ltar pha rol phyin lha mo//kha dog dmar me rnams gsal ma//zhal ni shin tu rnam 'gyur ba/
14a1(rgyud): cung zad mche ba gtsigs 'jigs ma//g.yas na cang te'u gri gug ste//g.yon na kha T+wAM thod pa'o//rang gi lus skyes 'od zer gyis/rtsa yi 'khor lo bskul bar bya//de yis bskul

14a6(rgyud): de ltar he ru ka bas ma nas//rnal 'byor ma ni brgyad kyis mchod//sna tshogs zas dang sna tshogs skom//sna tshogs rol mo mchog gsungs dang //dri zhim lnga dang me tog spos//'di dag gis ni gar+b+hadza
14a7(rgyud): mchod//mchod yon zhal bsil de bzhin khrus//gru yi mchog ni rnam mang pos//mgon mo khrag 'thung bdag nyid che//'di dag gis ni mchod par bya//dpa' bo rdzogs par mthong nas ni//rtsa yi 'jor/
14b1(rgyud): lolas ni 'dzag//'dzag pa de la sa rnal 'byor ma//rnam par brtse ba cher ldan pa//bde gshegs kun gyis byin rlabs ma//sna tshogs rgyan gyis rnam par klubs//sna tshogs pa yi na bza' branapas//gzugs
14b2(rgyud): denilang tsho gzhon pas rgyan//lo ni bcu dang gnyis lo par//phyag g.yas byang chub sems bka bang //bum pa amra'i lcug bcas bsnams//zhal ni rab bzhid dang ba yis//tsA ru ka ni rgyal ma /
14b3(rgyud): rgyal gyur cig ces 'di ltar smra//mgon pos mdun du bltas nas ni//dbang bskur mchog ste gsol ba gdab//rtse dang ldan pa'i grags chen mo//'khor ba'i 'dam du bying ba bdag/dbang bskor ba'i sa
14b4(rgyud): bdag sgrol phyir//rdo rje rnal 'byor mas khrus shig/dper na bu cha med pa'i khyim//shi ba tsam gyis stong pa nyid//de bzhin dbang dang bral na ni//ye shes kun gyi stongs pa nyid//dper nA pI dang sbyor kun
14b5(rgyud): tshogs//rgyud dang bral na rdung mi rung //de bzhin dbang dang bral na ni//sngags dang bsam gtan 'grub mi 'gyur//rmongs pa gang zhig dbang med par//bdag ni dbang bskur zhes smra ba//ji srid sangs rgyas
14b6(rgyud): bzhugs kyi bar//slob m+b+hir bcas te dmyal bar 'gro//de ltar shes bya rnal 'byor pas//slar yang bdag la dbang bskur cig/yang dang yang du phyag 'tsham te//thal mo sbyar nas gsol 'gags/
14b7(rgyud): gal te dbang bskung mi na ni//he ru ka ru bdag gyur cig/de nas rnal 'byor mdo rnams//rgyal gyur rgyal gyur zhes smre zhing //bcom ldan dbang bskur khrus gsol lo//phyi nang gsang bar bcas
15a1(rgyud): pa yi//dbang bskur tsam gyis na mkha' yi//dkyil nas rnga yi sgra grags cing //me tog can dan char 'bab 'gyur//de nas rnal 'byor ma de rnams//rtsa ba'i 'khor lo la ni
15a2(rgyud): thim//sangs rgyas thod pa'i rgyud rnal 'byor mi'i gong na med pa gsang ba'i yang shin tu gsang ba zhes bya ba las/lha bskyed pa dang /dbang bskur ba'i le'u ste gsum pa'o//

15a6(rgyud): lha mo bka' ni ci zhig gsol//kye lags ji lta bu zhig bgyi//gsungs pa/mu stegs la sogs mkha' lding sngags//ye shes las byung ji lta bu//dus su zin pa ji ltar yin//ji ltar drug ni skye
15a7(rgyud): bar 'gyur//sbrul gyis zin pa tsam gyis ni//slar yang sems cana'i cha 'gyur zhing //zhus pa/khyab 'jug dbang phyug sogs lha dang //tshangs pa tshangs pa 'dun na 'don//de rnams la ni 'chi 'pho
15b1(rgyud): 'ches//dug ni nyes pas gnod par 'gyur//de ltar dus su zin ces smras//sbrul gyi dug ni sel ba med//de bzhin sbrul la drug ni yod//sbrul zin 'tsho 'am mi 'tsho ba//bde byed la sogs rdzu 'phrul
15b2(rgyud): 'i//lha de rnams ni de ltar smra//stong pa stong nyid nges gsungs pa//bcom ldan rdo rje 'chang bas gsungs//chos rnams thams cad stong pa lo//sbrul gyi dug ni ji ltar spyod//gang gis 'dzin cing ga
15b3(rgyud): zhig 'dzin//dus dang dus min ji ltar 'gyur//ji ltar spyod cing ji lta bsdu//gang phyir 'dzin cing gang du 'dzin//sems can dug zin mi 'chi ba//stong nyid smra ba'i nges pa yi no//'dod chags gti mug stong
15b4(rgyud): pa nyid//grags chen yul ni stong pa nyid//yul gyi rang bzhin dri ma med//dri ma dang bral ji ltar dug/sbrul gyis kyang ni ci zhig byed//tha mal pa yi yul ni sbrul//yul gyi nyes pa drug nyid do//lha rnams
15b5(rgyud): yul rnams kyis ni bsgribs//thams cad dus su zin pa yin//yul gyi nyes pa sbyangs pa nyid//stong pa longs spyod gos mi 'gyur//sangs rgyas thod pa'i rnal 'byor pas//'dod kun nye bar longs spyod bya//
15b6(rgyud): re skags sbyor ba rnyod dka' dang //sangs rgyas thod pa'i sbyor ldan pas//'dir ni klu rnams thams cad lhags//de phyir rob des lha mo kye//dus zin the tsom med pa ru//blo med mu stegs can de smra//'di ltar smras
15b7(rgyud): te klu rnams kyis//sna tshogs sde la phyag 'tshal te//ring rang gi ni gnas su dong //de nas bcom ldan 'das mas yul gyi nyes pa smong ba'i sngags gsungs pa//oM shU n+ya tA dz+nyA na badz+ra swa b+hA wa At+ma ko haM3//s+thA
16a1(rgyud): /sa sa sa/rlu la sa / b+hU sasgyu // sas sa// rgyun du na na
16a2(rgyud): dag pa chen pos bcom ldan 'das ma'i nabs la skyibs gtugs te/'di skad ces gsol to//ri sa ba rnyed da//'a ba//lham yin pa byangad dru gastsal//sems can dan la gcig tu 'bar/

22b1(rgyud): bud med gang //kha dag nag mos rab mdzes ma//gang du thabs shes gnyis 'dus pa//de yi kha sbyar sbyor las byung //sman de'i ming ni grub mar bshad//sangs rgyas thod pa'i sbyor ba yis//bud//
22b2(rgyud): med rab mdzes ma nyams dang //dbang po gnyis kyi sbyor ba yis//mi phyed nye bar spyad pa yi//de la dang por byung ba'i rdzas//sman de byis pa can no zhes//bdag nyid chen po'i lho mos gsungs//
22b3(rgyud): lhan cig skyes dgur byung ba'i rdzas//byang chub sems mchog chen mar khu//chags pa yi chu dag dang ni//bsre 'gyur 'di ni the tsom med//sman de'i ming ni thod can ma'o//zla ba nyi ma'i sbyor ba yis//
22b4(rgyud): bya bar 'dir ni the tshom med//zla bas zla bar nyi mas nyir//de lus skra dkar gnyer ma zhi//ji srid sangs rgyas bzhugs kyi bar//de yi tshe nI sangs rgyas 'gyur//sman 'di grub pa tsami gyis ni/
22b5(rgyud): dgeg pa'i lus su 'byung bar 'gyur//dngos po gang dang gang yang rung //lcags dang zangs ma'i snod dag sa//dngul ni byugs pa nam gyis ni//dngul dang gser du 'gyur ba yin//de nas yang dag
22b6(rgyud): rlub bshad pa//dgongs bshad shin tu rnyed dka' ba//rgyud gnan du ni rab smras pa//'badu bas de 'di de rab gsal bya//dri zhu yo shes rdo rje ste//dri rten rdo rje bzang po nyid//khrag ni mar me rdo rje
22b7(rgyud): yin//khru brdo rje'i baba' byung nyid//shin chos kyi rje yin//de ldan la 'byor ma yi mchog/gang shi dmachog rnyed dade/'angagi/bas 'di bdag gis bshad par bya//ba'ang shini 'phang ba ste//
23a1(rgyud): /Sh+ya yi sha la spyo bar gsum//rta ye shel bza' bar bshad//glang po'i shul zhu bar gsungs//shachen ma ni bzang por bshad//de lta rnal 'byung mdzug tu bsungs
23a2(rgyud): rnal 'byor ma la de ldan par//gal te gcig tu byed nus pa//de tshe rnam rtog de thams cad//'jig 'gyur 'dir ni the tshom med//zin la bsod nams zhes bya ste//tshod ma la ni sdig pa nyid//rnal
23a3(rgyud): 'byor shin tu rnyed dka' gsungs//byis pa la ni 'gal ba nyid//g.yungs mo la ni bzang mor gsungs//rus pa'i phreng la rdzas zhes bya//skyes bu la ni rdo rjer gsungs//bud med la ni snod//
23a4(rgyud): bzang nyid//dbang po gnyis kyi rab sbyong la//gzi brjid phreng chen de bshad do//rab chags shin tu mthong ba nyid//'khyud pa la ni chos zhes brjod//'dri ba lnga ni mar me'o//shin tu 'di
23a5(rgyud): me zhes bya//'gro ba la ni phreng can ma//'od la shin tu phreng can mo//myur ba la ni byug ces bya//dpa' ba la ni bzang de brjod//pad+ma rtsa 'jo phreng can ma//sngags kyi sa mtshan la rab nges zhe'o//
23a6(rgyud): ldag la lte 'og ces bya ste//so la bza' ba sna la bde//mig la rol rtsed mu tig rna//gsang ba'i yul la rnyed dka' zhe'o//'od dag bshad do lag chen po//'jig rten gsum na rab rnyed
23a7(rgyud): dka'//sangs rgyas thod pa'i rnal 'byor pa//med par phan tshun smra mi bya//'on kyang bshad chen de nyid 'di//gcig la gcig gi smra bar bya//rgyud rnams thams cad du sbas pa//rgyud
23b1(rgyud): 'dUr+ya na bstsal bar byas//nye 'dun grong mtha' lhan cig zhe'o//'dus pa phyi rol zhes su gsungs//nye ba'i 'dus pa nang de bzhin//gnas la 'bras bu zhes su gsungs//nye ba'i gnas la shing
23b2(rgyud): ni//grongs pa'i la nis tsan+da gi s+t+rai ka//nye ba'i grong ma' byaga'o//tshogs pa lan nga ngur gsungs//gcig pu la ni 'dab ma ste//snying ba la ni rtsa bzhi'o//de ltar dgangs pas bshad pa
23b3(rgyud): na//bde da shegs rnams byas mi mkhyen no//spyan ma la stsogs rnal 'byor ma//rnams kyi khong du mi chud cing //byang chub sems dpa'i yul min zhing //bla ma gus pa'i rnal 'byor pas/
23b4(rgyud): spros pa thams cad spangs nas ni//rdzas la chags pa mi bya'o//shin tu stong sgom rnal 'byor pa//'dod chags zhe sdang phrag dog med//gti mug dang ni nga rgyal spangs//nyon mongs thams cad rnam
23b5(rgyud): par spangs//za 'thung de bzhin glu lan na//shin tu spros pa spring bar bya//bde bas dga' bo nyid dang ni//shes rab thebs kyis bdag nyid gsungs//bla med de nyid zla phyed kyis//'grub par the tshom
23b6(rgyud): med pa'o//kyai lags grags mi 'groklan gang //mtha' dag drim med pa yi//blta dang bral la skye ba lngas//gsag gsapa rang bzhin brdzun sgrub//pad+ma ma grib rgyu lta bur ltos//dbang po lnga ni sgra
23b7(rgyud): zhing //lnga phung dag pa'i rang bzhin gyi//rnal 'byur 'di ni bsgoms pas 'brug//sangs rgyas zad pa'i rdul 'byor ma'i gong na me pa gsang ba'i yang shin tu gseng po zhes bya ba las smra dzin//
24a1(rgyud): /bzang ba dang//dgongs pas bshad pa'i le'u ste lnga padz+ra///de nas yang drug rab bshad pa//dkyil 'khor 'jigs pa mchog gsang bar//thabs dang
24a2(rgyud): shes rab sgrub pa yin//gang gis slob ma dbang bskur ba//shes rab pad+ma'i nang dbus su//dpag tshad bye ba'i dkyil 'khor la//gsum rtseg dag pa'i bdag nyid lus//'khor ba'i 'jigs
24a3(rgyud): pa las skyob pa//dkyil 'khor de yi dbus gnas par//mkhas pas slob ma bzang po bskur//gal te byang chub bla med 'dod//phyi yi dkyil 'khor bya ba min//lha rnams bshigs
24a4(rgyud): pa tsam gyis ni//sdig pa chen po skye bar 'gyur//des na rdul tshon tsam gyis ni//de bzhin lha rnams dag mi 'gyur//rdo rje 'khor mi rin chen dang //de bzhin pad+ma ral gri nyid//byas nas
24a5(rgyud): slar yang 'jig byed pa//skyes bu tha shal dmyal bar 'gro//gang gis sangs rgyas spyan drangs shing //gang gis gshegs su gsol ba yis//rdo rje sems dpa' byon pa dang //de bzhin
24a6(rgyud): gshegs pa byin pa rnams//gang na'ang byon pa ma yin no//dri ma med cing dag pa'i lus//gang gis spyan drangs gshegs su gsol//de nyid kyis ni rtag med par//de bzhin gshegs pa
24a7(rgyud): rnams phyag bya//lo bcu gnyis pa'i bu mo ni//tshul khrims mnyams chags mu ma'o//thos dang ljon zhing brags can mAM//shand med snying rje dang ldan ma//sems can don la gcig
24b1(rgyud): nan tan//rgod cing pad+ma'i spyan dang ldan//zla ba'i cha 'dra gdong mdzes ma//mu cor mi smra brtan zhing dul//des na slob ma blo chen po//shin tu dad pa'i sems dang ldan//'dod med dbang po dul ba
24b2(rgyud): dang //chags dang cha gas bral rnam par spangs//sems can don la shin tu sbyor//gti mug zhe sdang phrag dog spangs//sangs rgyas kun gyis byin gyis brlabs//de rnams la ni de nyid
24b3(rgyud): bshad//gsang ba phyi yi lnga dang ni//bdun dang bcu bzhir bshad pa dang //gnyis ka cig tu 'dus pa'o//gsang ba'i de nyid bshad par bya//slob ma legs dang ldan pa dang //brtse ldan
24b4(rgyud): sems gzhan med pa yis//gser ni 'bum phrag bcu drug dang //sa gzhi yul 'khor ldan pa dang //glang po bud med dam pa dang //ral gri 'khor lo rta dang ni//yongs 'dren skyes bu rin
24b5(rgyud): chen rnams//sbyor dang ldan pa'i sems kyis ni//der ni bla ma dbul bar bya//shin tu dri med sems kyis ni//de nas 'dir ni gsol ba dang //'khor ba'i 'dam du bying ba dag/dpung gnyen
24b6(rgyud): khyod byas bsgral du gsol//bdag ni rtsol chung skal dman zhing //sangs rgyas chas ni rnam par spangs//kye kye ston pa bla ma che//mgon po khyod kyis brtse bar mdzad//de ltar gsol
24b7(rgyud): 'debs tshig gis na nas//de ru bla ma mi gsung bzhugs//man ngag 'di yi cha dag ni//glegs bam rnams las spyod yul yin//dkyil 'khor gang la gang gis rgyan//mtshan ma'i don
25a1(rgyud): gan gar bgad //su lis sangs rgyas spyan drangs kyi//'gro ba brnyan tshwa'o sa mnyer snang //mtha' dag stong pa gros med //rgyu nang thub ci 'drag
25a2(rgyud): dra'i dkyil 'khor bde dbus gnas//kya lags rnal 'byor ma tshogs ltos//der ni he ru ka gcig dang //thams cad bskyed par byed ma yin//'gro kun rmi lam skye bas na/
25a3(rgyud): gti mug las ni bskyed pa skyes//sangs rgyas thod pa'i rgyud rnal 'byor ma'i gong na med pa gsang ba'i yang shin tu gsang ba las dkyil 'khor 'jigs pa bri ba dang //slob ma
25a4(rgyud): dbang bskur ba'i le'u ste drug pa'o///de nas yang dag rab bshad pa//ri dang phug dang tshad tshing ngam//yang na dur khrod dag dang ni//gdod nas grub pa'i
25a5(rgyud): gnas su 'am//'on te rgya mtsho'i 'gram dag tu//phyi yi dkyil 'khor bla med bri//rdul tshon sngon po ni ro bsregs pa'i sol ba las bya'o//rdul tshon dmar po ni dur khrod
25a6(rgyud): kyi so phag las bya'o//rdul tshon ljang ku ni nim pa'i 'dab ma las bya'o//rdul tshon dkar po ni mi'i rus pa'i phye ma las bya'o//rdul tshon ser po ni yung ba'i phye ma las bya'o//
25a7(rgyud): deltar rdul chen lnga rnams kyis//mkhas pas dkyil 'khor bri bar bya//pho brang rigs gsum zlum po la//rdo rje gsum gyis yongs su bskor//phyi rol gru bzhi
25b1(rgyud): sgrim pa po//sgo shir rta babs kyis rgyun pa//ba dan rnam pa bzhi yis rgyan//dra ba drub phyed pas smras//phyi rol khwa lce rag pa dang //rin chen pha gung yang dag ldan//pad+ma
25b2(rgyud): nyi shu lnga'i//ga na rnams kyis ni shin tu mdzes//de yi dbus chung sa bon ni//yi ge hU~M gi rang bzhin sngo//skad cig can gyis he ru ka/sku mdog sngon po brags chen po/
25b3(rgyud): ng+yas de bang te'u gri thub ste//g.yon na kha nI thod pa'o//skyil krung byed pas 'jigs chen po//zhal gyi mche ba cung zad gtsigs//ral ba'i cod pan gyis rkyen cing //sangs rgyas
25b4(rgyud): yi rgod pan can//dbul sna tshogs rdo rje mnan//zla ba byeng ba 'dzin pa'i lha//sku la thal ba'i rdul gyis byugs//dpa' bo phyag 'i phyag mtshan 'chang //shin tu hUM grogs 'jigs
25b5(rgyud): byed pa//gang gyi sgrubs kyis rnam par bzhugs//mgo bo rlon pa'i phreng ba can//mchod phyir thogs pa 'tshong ba zo//thod pa gti drug rlom dag pa//skyeng ba brgyus pas rgyan pa'i lha/
